PUSHBYTEFSREGREGPLUSV X Y Z
&I=^DIV_IDIV_BYTE
POPDWORDREG MY2
POPDWORDREG MY1
=>
*I*FSREGREGPLUSV X Y Z

PUSHDWORDREG MY2
